               rymQ(window.ui.section_nav._initPage);
            }
            </script>

         <script>

           window.addEventListener('load', (event) => {

               for ( var i in window.ryminit ) {
                  var fn = window.ryminit[i];
                  window.ryminit[i] = null;
                  if ( fn ) {
                     fn();
                  }
               }

               window.ryminit = null;
            });

         </script>
